    return false;

    }
    return false;
  }

  }

  return true;

        == tot - (a + b + c)
        == n;
  }

  return true;
}

method CollectingCoins(a: int, b: int, c: int, n: int) returns (result: bool)
  requires a >= 0 && b >= 0 && c >= 0 && n >= 0
  ensures result == CanDistribute(a, b, c, n)
{

  if tot % 3 != 0 {
    // No valid distribution exists when total is not divisible by 3
    return false;
  }
  var des := tot / 3;
  if a > des || b > des || c > des {
    // If any pile already exceeds the target, distribution is impossible
    return false;

  assert (des - a) + (des - b) + (des - c) == n;
  return true;

  requires a >= 0 && b >= 0 && c >= 0 && n >= 0

{

    forall A: int, B: int, C: int
      ensures !ValidDistribution(a, b, c, n, A, B, C)
    {
      if A >= 0 && B >= 0 && C >= 0 && A + B + C == n && a + A == b + B && a + A == c + C {
        assert 3 * (a + A) == tot;
      }
    }
    return false;
  }
  var des := tot / 3;
  if a > des || b > des || c > des {
    forall A: int, B: int, C: int
      ensures !ValidDistribution(a, b, c, n, A, B, C)
    {
      if A >= 0 && B >= 0 && C >= 0 && A + B + C == n && a + A == b + B && a + A == c + C {
        assert 3 * (a + A) == tot;
        assert tot == 3 * des;
        assert a + A == des;
      }
    }
    return false;
  }
  assert (des - a) + (des - b) + (des - c) == n by {
    assert 3 * des == tot;
    assert (des - a) + (des - b) + (des - c) == 3 * des - (a + b + c);
    assert 3 * des - (a + b + c) == tot - (a + b + c);
    assert tot - (a + b + c) == n;
  }

  return true;
}
